2024-03-23T17:28:27Z #11 301.9 variables OMPI_MCA_pml="ucx" OMPI_MCA_osc="ucx" before launching your MPI processes.
2024-03-23T17:28:27Z #11 301.9 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameters in the command line:
2024-03-23T17:28:27Z #11 301.9 mpiexec --mca pml ucx --mca osc ucx ...
